"බීජවල බලය තිෙයන්ෙන් කාටද? ඔහු කෘෂිකර්මය ෙලොව පුරා පාලනය කරයි". එය තමයි ඇත්ත. අද විශාල අස්වැන්නක් ලබා ෙදන බීජ වර්ග අපට එවනවා. ඒ වාෙග්ම ඒ අස්වැන්න -වීවල ෙනොෙවයි- සෑම ෙදයකම වාෙග් ෙගොවිතැනින් ලැෙබන්නා වූ අස්වැන්න නැත්නම් ඒ බීජවලින් ලැෙබන ඵල ඇත්තටම ඉතා විෙශේෂ ගුණාංගයන්ෙගන් සමන්විතයි. ෙලෙහසිෙයන් තැෙළන්ෙන් ෙපොඩි ෙවන්ෙන් නැහැ. තක්කාලි, පැෙපොල් ෙලෙහසිෙයන් කුණු ෙවන්ෙන් නැහැ; ඉෙදන්ෙන් නැහැ. ඒ නිසා එම බීජ වර්ගවලට අද ෙගොදුරු වීමක් තිෙබනවා. හැබැයි ඒ බීජවල එක ගතියක් තිෙබනවා. ඒ බීජවලින් හැෙදන ෙගඩියකින් ආපසු බීජ ගන්න බැහැ. ඒවාට කියන්ෙන් "terminators" කියලායි. ෙම්වා දැන් ඔක්ෙකොම වාෙග් දන්නවා. "Terminators" කියන්ෙන් එතැනින් ඉවරයි. ඒ බීජ ෙගනාවා; එයින් යමක් හදා වඩා ගත්තා; ඒක කෑවා; එතැනින් ඉවරයි. ඒෙකන් බීජයක් අරෙගන ආපසු පැළ කරන්න බැහැ.

අෙප් ජනාධිපතිතුමා පසු ගිය අය වැෙය්දී කිව්වා, ෙම් බීජ පිළිබඳ පශ්නය අපට බරපතළයි කියලා. හැම ෙදයකම බීජ -ලූනු ෙව්වා, අල ෙව්වා- පිළිබඳ පර්ෙය්ෂණ කරන්න අෙප් විද්‍යාඥෙයෝ ෙයොදා ගත්ත අෙප් රජෙය් බීජ ෙගොවිෙපොළවල් එක්සත් ජාතික පක්ෂෙය් ආණ්ඩුව කාලෙය් එක එක ෙපෞද්ගලික සමාගම්වලට හා එක එක ෙපෞද්ගලික ෙපොෙහොසතුන්ට විකුණා දැමුවා. අෙප් බීජ නිෂ්පාදනය, බීජ පර්ෙය්ෂණය සම්පූර්ණෙයන්ම අකා මකා දැමූ ඒ කාලෙයන් මිදිලා නැවතත් බීජ පර්ෙය්ෂණයට අෙප් බීජ ෙගොවිෙපොළවල් නැවතත් පුනරුත්ථාපනය කර ඒවා නඟා හිටුවා අලුත්ම බීජ වර්ග නිපදවා ගන්න කටයුතු කිරීමට අෙප් ජනාධිපතිතුමාෙග් අය වැෙයන් ෙමවර මුදල් ෙවන් කළා. ෙමන්න බීජ පිළිබඳ තත්ත්වය බලන්න.

කියුබාව ආහාරවලින් ඉතාමත්ම අසීරු තත්ත්වයකයි හිටිෙය්. ඇයි? ඒ රෙට් ආහාර වැව්ෙව් නැහැ. උක් වැව්ෙව්. නමුත් ඉතා ඉක්මනින්ම ඒ රෙට් කෘෂිකර්මය ආහාර ෙභෝග වගාවට ගියා. ඒ අයෙග් විද්‍යාඥයන් හරහා ඒ අය අෙප් මුං ඇට වාෙග් යම් බීජ වර්ග ෙසොයා ගත්තා. ඒ බීජවලින්ම ෙපොෙළොව ෙපොෙහොර ෙවනවා. අලුතින් ෙපොෙහොර ෙයොදන්න වුවමනාවක් නැහැ. ෙපොෙළොව ෙපොෙහොර ෙවන බීජ වර්ග නිර්මාණය කර ෙගන -පර්ෙය්ෂණ කරෙගන හදා ෙගන- ෙපොෙළොව සරු කර ෙගන ඒ මඟින් ඔවුන්ෙග් රෙට් ආහාර පශ්නය විසඳා ගන්න ඔවුන්ට පුළුවන් වුණා. අපි අන්න එවැනි ෙද්වල් ආදර්ශයට ගත යුතු ෙවනවා. බීජ පිළිබඳ වගකීම රජය සතු විය යුතුයි. බීජවල බලය රජය අෙත් තිෙබන්න ඕනෑ. එය සමාජය ෙවනුෙවන්, සමාජෙය් භාරයක් හැටියට තිෙබන්න ඕනෑ. ඒ නිසා බීජ පර්ෙය්ෂණය, නව බීජ වර්ග

1239 1240

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව

නිපදවා ගැනීම, ෙම් රටට හුරු පරණ බීජ වර්ග අලුත් සංවර්ධනයකට ගැනීම, පරණ බීජ අලුතින් සංවර්ධනය කිරීෙම් පර්ෙය්ෂණවල ෙයදීම වැනි කටයුතු එක්ක අෙප් වී වගාව සම්බන්ධ වී තිෙබනවා. වී වගා කිරීෙම්, වී ෙකටීෙම් ඉඳලා ෙවෙළඳ ෙපොළට හාල් නිකුත් කිරීම දක්වා රජය මැදිහත් වීෙම් කියා දාමයක් තිෙබනවා. එමඟින් නිෂ්පාදනය සමාජෙය් යහපතට වුවමනා විධියට හරවන්න නිෂ්පාදකයාත්, ඒ වාෙග්ම පාරිෙභෝගිකයාත් යම් ආකාරයක මිල පිළිබඳ තුලනාත්මක ස්ථාවරත්වයක තැබීමට අෙප් රජය කටයුතු කරෙගන යනවා. මම හිතනවා, මම කතා කළා ඇතිය කියා. ෙම් කරුණු ෙබොෙහෝ ෙසේ විහිදී යනවා. ආහාර පිළිබඳ කරුණු එක පැත්තකට විහිෙදනවා. අපිම නිපද වන අෙප් හාල්වල, අෙප් වීවල cadmium කියන බැර ෙලෝහ වර්ගෙය් සාන්දණය oxidize වී අඩංගු වීම නිසා එහි තිෙබන්නා වූ හානිය ගැන බැලිය යුතු ෙවනවා. ඒ වාෙග්ම ආහාර සුරක්ෂිතතාව ෙවනුෙවන් අෙප් රජය දැවැන්ත පියවරක් අරෙගන තිෙබනවා. නටබුන් කර දමා තිෙබන අපෙග් විශාල හාල් ෙමෝල් නැවතත් ජීවමාන කරලා ෙම් රෙට් කෘෂිකර්මෙය් දියුණුව තවත් ඉදිරියට ෙගන ෙගොස් ෙලෝකය ආහාර අර්බුදයකට මුහණ ෙදන ෙකොට ෙම් පුංචි ශී ලංකාව ආහාර පිළිබඳ තමන්ෙග් පශ්නය විසඳා ගත්ත රටක් හැටියට ඒ ෙලෝකෙය් ආසියාෙව් ආශ්චර්යයට එකතු ෙවන්න පුළුවන්ය කියමින් මෙග් වචන ස්වල්පය අවසන් කරනවා.

පශ්නය විමසන ලදින්, සභා සම්මත විය. පනත් ෙකටුම්පත ඊට අනුකූලව ෙදවන වර කියවන ලදී.

வினா விᾌக்கப்பட்ᾌ, ஏற்ᾠக் ெகாள்ளப்பட்டᾐ. அதன்பᾊ, சட்டᾚலம் இரண்டாம் ᾙைறயாக மதிப்பிடப்பட்டᾐ. Question put, and agreed to. Bill accordingly read a Second time.

මතු පළවන ෙයෝජනාව සභා සම්මත විය:

''පනත් ෙකටුම්පත පූර්ණ පාර්ලිෙම්න්තු කාරක සභාවකට පැවරිය යුතු ය.'' --[ගරු වාසුෙද්ව නානායක්කාර මහතා]

தீர்மானிக்கப்பட்டᾐ. "சட்டᾚலம் ᾙᾨப் பாராᾦமன்றக் குᾨᾫக்குச் சாட்டப்பᾌமாக" [மாண்ᾗமிகு வாசுேதவ நாணாயக்கார] Resolved: "That the Bill be referred to a Committee of the whole Parliament." - [The Hon. Vasudeva Nanayakkara]

කාරක සභාෙවහිදී සලකා බලන ලදී. [නිෙයෝජ්‍ය කථානායකතුමා මූලාසනාරූඪ විය.] குᾨவில் ஆராயப்பட்டᾐ. [பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கள் தைலைம வகித்தார்கள்.] Considered in Committee. [MR. DEPUTY SPEAKER in the Chair.]

1 සිට 3 ෙතක් වගන්ති පනත් ෙකටුම්පෙතහි ෙකොටසක් හැටියට තිබිය යුතු යයි නිෙයෝග කරන ලදී.

1ஆம் வாசகத்திᾢᾞந்ᾐ 3ஆம் வாசகம் வைர சட்டᾚலத்தின் பகுதியாக இᾞக்க ேவண்ᾌெமனக் கட்டைளயிடப்பட்டᾐ. Clauses 1 to 3 ordered to stand part of the Bill.

පඥප්ති වගන්තිය සහ නාමය පනත් ෙකටුම්පෙතහි ෙකොටසක් හැටියට තිබිය යුතුයයි නිෙයෝග කරන ලදී. පනත් ෙකටුම්පත, සංෙශෝධන රහිතව වාර්තා කරන ලදී.

சட்டமாகு வாசகᾙம் தைலப்ᾗம் சட்டᾚலத்தின் பகுதியாக இᾞக்க ேவண்ᾌெமனக் கட்டைளயிடப்பட்டᾐ. சட்டᾚலம் திᾞத்தமின்றி அறிக்ைக ெசய்யப்பட்டᾐ. Enacting Clause and Title ordered to stand part of the Bill.Bill reported without Amendments.

ගරු වාසුෙද්ව නානායක්කාර මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு வாசுேதவ நாணாயக்கார) (The Hon. Vasudeva Nanayakkara) ගරු නිෙයෝජ්‍ය කථානායකතුමනි, "පනත් ෙකටුම්පත දැන් තුන්වන වර කියවිය යුතුය" යි මා ෙයෝජනා කරනවා.

පශ්නය විමසන ලදින්, සභා සම්මත විය. පනත් ෙකටුම්පත ඊට අනුකූලව තුන්වන වර කියවා සම්මත කරන ලදී.

வினா விᾌக்கப்பட்ᾌ, ஏற்ᾠக் ெகாள்ளப்பட்டᾐ. அதன்பᾊ, சட்டᾚலம் ᾚன்றாம் ᾙைறயாக மதிப்பிடப்பட்ᾌ நிைறேவற்றப்பட்டᾐ. Question put, and agreed to. Bill accordingly read the Third time, and passed.

වී අෙලවි මණ්ඩලය පනත: ෙයෝජනාව

ெநற் சந்ைதப்பᾌத்தல் சைபச் சட்டம்: ஒᾨங்குவிதிகள் PADDY MARKETING BOARD ACT: REGULATIONS

ගරු වාසුෙද්ව නානායක්කාර මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு வாசுேதவ நாணாயக்கார) (The Hon. Vasudeva Nanayakkara) Sir, on behalf of the Minister of Co-operatives and Internal Trade, I move, “That the Regulations made by the Minister of Co-operatives and Internal Trade under Section 62 read with Section 10 and paragraph (6) of Section 4 of the Paddy Marketing Board Act, No. 14 of 1971, and published in the Gazette Extraordinary No. 1684/54 of December 18th, 2010, which was presented on 24.02.2011, be approved. (Cabinet approval signified)" පශ්නය විමසන ලදින්, සභා සම්මත විය. வினா விᾌக்கப்பட்ᾌ ஏற்ᾠக்ெகாள்ளப்பட்டᾐ. Question put, and agreed to.

කල්තැබීම ஒத்திைவப்ᾗ ADJOURNMENT ගරු සාලින්ද දිසානායක මහතා (ෙද්ශීය ෛවද්‍ය අමාත්‍යතුමා)

(மாண்ᾗமிகு சாᾢந்த திசாநாயக்க - சுேதச மᾞத்ᾐவத்ᾐைற அைமச்சர்) (The Hon. Salinda Dissanayake - Minister of Indigenous Medicine) ගරු නිෙයෝජ්‍ය කථානායකතුමනි, "පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව දැන් කල් තැබිය යුතුය" යි මා ෙයෝජනා කරනවා.

පශ්නය සභාභිමුඛ කරන ලදී. வினா எᾌத்தியம்பப்ெபற்றᾐ. Question proposed.

නිෙයෝජ්‍ය කථානායකතුමා (பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கள்) (The Deputy Speaker) Before the Adjournment Motion is moved by the Hon. (Prof.) Rajiva Wijesinha, will an Hon. Member propose the Hon. Alhaj A.H.M. Azwer to take the Chair?

ගරු වාසුෙද්ව නානායක්කාර මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு வாசுேதவ நாணாயக்கார) (The Hon. Vasudeva Nanayakkara) I propose that the Hon. Alhaj A.H.M. Azwer do now take the Chair.

1241 1242

[ගරු වාසුෙද්ව නානායක්කාර මහතා]

2011 අෙපේල් 06

පශ්නය විමසන ලදින්, සභා සම්මත විය. வினா விᾌக்கப்பட்ᾌ ஏற்ᾠக்ெகாள்ளப்பட்டᾐ. Question put, and agreed to. අනතුරුව නිෙයෝජ්‍ය කථානායකතුමා මූලාසනෙයන් ඉවත් වූෙයන්, ගරු අල්හාජ් ඒ.එච්.එම්. අස්වර් මහතා මූලාසනාරූඪ විය.

அதன் பிறகு, பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கள் அக்கிராசனத்தினின்ᾠ அகலேவ, மாண்ᾗமிகு அல்ஹாஜ் ஏ.எச்.எம். அஸ்வர் அவர்கள் தைலைம வகித்தார்கள். Whereupon MR. DEPUTY SPEAKER left the Chair, and THE HON. ALHAJ A.H.M. AZWER took the Chair.

මූලාසනාරූඪ මන්තීතුමා (தைலைமதாங்கும் உᾠப்பினர் அவர்கள்) (The Presiding Member) Hon. (Prof.) Rajiva Wijesinha, you may now move the Adjournment Motion.

ආරුමුගම් ෙත්වරාජන් මහතාට මහ රැජින සම්මානයක් පිරිනැමීම පිළිබඳව කනස්සල්ල திᾞ. ஆᾠᾙகம் ேதவராஜᾔக்கு மகாராணி விᾞᾐ வழங்கப்பட்டைம பற்றி வᾞத்தம் ெதாிவித்தல் DISPLEASURE OVER QUEEN'S AWARD TO MR. ARUMUGAM THEVARAJAN

ගරු මහාචාර්ය රාජීව විෙජ්සිංහ මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேபராசிாியர் ராஜீவ விேஜசிங்க) (The Hon. (Prof.) Rajiva Wijesinha) Sir, it is with some sorrow that I move,

“That this House do stand adjourned to express its surprise that the Government of New Zealand saw fit to honour Mr. Arumugam Thevarajan, a member of the so-called Transitional Government of Tamil Eelam , in the recent New Year Awards presented by the Queen; to regret that such an award was conferred upon an individual pursuing a separatist agenda during a post-conflict situation in Sri Lanka where reconciliation between all communities is of paramount importance; to appreciate the prompt reaction of Sri Lanka in providing assistance to New Zealand following the disastrous Christchurch earthquake; to acknowledge the positive trade relations between New Zealand and Sri Lanka and recognize that this contributes nearly $300 million each year to the New Zealand economy, mainly through the export of milk powder to Sri Lanka by Fonterraa; and to urge the Ministry of External Affairs not only to raise Sri Lankan concerns with the Government of New Zealand but also to ensure prompt replies to these concerns, inasmuch as the positive relations between the peoples of the two countries should not be adversely affected by insensitive indulgence of a separatist agenda".

I am sorry, Mr. Presiding Member, because I had thought that relations between our countries were at a level which ensured sensitivity to the concerns of the other. It was worrying therefore to see the New Zealand Government nominating an avowed separatist, associated with the excesses of a terrorist group and its successors, for such a great honour.

I say "great honour", because New Zealand is undoubtedly a country, apart from the United Kingdom, in which an honour from the Queen is taken most seriously. Mr. Arumugam Thevarajan, who is one of the two members representing New Zealand in the so-called

Transitional Government of Tamil Eelam, was given the Queen’s Service Medal, for which he must have been nominated by the current New Zealand Government. Not at all surprisingly, neither to us nor to that Government, he took advantage of the honour to inform the media that “What is happening in Sri Lanka is not war or even riot - it is genocide”.

The TamilNet article in which the account of Mr. Thevarajan and his politicking appeared, mentioned that two other Tamils had been honoured in the British New Year Honours. Neither seems to have been involved in separatism, and I believe that we too as Sri Lankans can be proud of the contribution to education of Mr. Yogamoorthy, who was born and educated in Sri Lanka like Mr. Thevarajan. Mr. Yogamoorthy was a graduate of Peradeniya and has used the skills he obtained through our free education system to shine as an Engineer in England, to the extent of being able to lecture even to the British Army on the Rhine.

The other person to receive an MBE was Lakshmi Holmstrom, who was originally from India. TamilNet suggests support for their cause by nothing that she has translated “…. a good number of Eezham Tamil poetry into English”, but Ms. Holmstrom is simply an excellent scholar who has done much for Tamil literature in general. While her sympathies for Tamil people are understandable, as those of many of us in this House, I do not think she would ever lend support to terrorism.

If Britain then has been circumspect, in spite - I am sure - of pressures from those hangers-on in the last British Parliament who furthered a terrorist cause for electoral advantage, it is doubly sad that New Zealand has failed to live up to the ideals we both share as democratic countries. We have shown our sympathy for their suffering after the recent earthquake and we must congratulate our diplomatic and consular officials for their prompt action in this regard. I hope too that we will also continue to make more tangible and continuous benefits to the New Zealand economy through our passion for their milk powder. I personally feel that this is an area in which successful marketing has triumphed over health considerations, but I do not think even those who agree with me about the disadvantages of powdered milk would consider trying to reduce the trade gap between our countries. It would be nice, though I should add, if New Zealand too were to help us to improve our own dairy industry in the North. This is, I think, being done by more active supporters of Sri Lanka such as the Netherlands, but perhaps New Zealand too would consider such assistance in a field in which they have profited from us so successfully in the past.

Given our good relations, Mr. Presiding Member, I cannot believe that New Zealand could have deliberately engaged in actions that lend strength to proponents of separatism and terrorism. It is possible that they have not

1243 1244

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව

been adequately briefed about the situation. In this regard, I believe it important that our Ministry of External Affairs make it clear to its counterpart that we are deeply hurt. We should not only protest through our High Commission in Australia, which is, I believe, accredited to New Zealand too, but we should also make contact with the New Zealand High Commissioner to Sri Lanka who is based in Delhi.

I should note that the High Commission there has seemed to me sensitive about Sri Lankan concerns.

I was able to assist the High Commissioner a couple of years ago about a consular question with which he was deeply but very practically concerned. Later, our own High Commission in Delhi, which maintained good contacts with high professionalism with their counterparts there, arranged a very positive meeting for me when I visited them, at a time when there was some unfair criticism of Sri Lanka by other countries.

But, I think it is important too that we should make clear our concerns, diplomatically and quietly but definitely. For too long, Mr. Presiding Member, we have allowed feelings to be built up against us which we have ignored following which we tend to react dramatically when problems arise. I, myself have in the past advocated that we should call in people when difficulties begin and quietly make clear our position. I believe we have every right to deplore support for separatism and to expect that friendly nations refrain from providing implicit encouragement to the remnants of the Tiger caravan. That picked up a lot of decent people in what seemed its relentless march to success from 2001 onwards. Now that we have dealt with that, we must also teach friendly countries to help us to wean such people away from violence and terror and encourage them to join us in the great efforts we are making to promote resettlement, rehabilitation and reconciliation.

In such a context, the insensitive approach of the New Zealand Government will not help. I hope we can ensure that such regrettable actions will not recur. Thank you.

මූලාසනාරූඪ මන්තීතුමා (தைலைமதாங்கும் உᾠப்பினர் அவர்கள்)

(The Presiding Member) Thank you, Hon. Member. This Adjournment Motion will be seconded by the Hon. Shehan Semasinghe.

ගරු ෙශහාන් ෙසේමසිංහ මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ெசஹான் ேசமசிங்க) (The Hon. Shehan Semasinghe) මූලාසනාරූඪ ගරු මන්තීතුමනි, මා එම ෙයෝජනාව ස්ථිර කරනවා.

මූලාසනාරූඪ මන්තීතුමා (தைலைமதாங்கும் உᾠப்பினர் அவர்கள்) (The Presiding Member) Hon. Dilan Perera, please. ගරු ඩිලාන් ෙපෙර්රා මහතා (විෙද්ශ රැකියා පවර්ධන හා සුබ සාධන අමාත්‍යතුමා)

(மாண்ᾗமிகு ᾊலான் ெபேரரா - ெவளிநாட்ᾌ ேவைலவாய்ப்ᾗ ஊக்குவிப்ᾗ, நலேனாம்ᾗைக அைமச்சர்) (The Hon. Dilan Perera - Minister of Foreign Employment Promotion and Welfare) Mr. Presiding Member, I thank you for permitting me the Floor to respond to the Adjournment Motion moved by the Hon. (Prof.) Rajiva Wijesinha and seconded by the Hon. Shehan Semasinghe. I do so in my capacity as the Acting Minister of External Affairs in the absence of the Hon. (Prof.) G.L. Peiris, Minister of External Affairs.

The issue of recognition accorded to Mr. Arumugam Thevarajan by the New Zealand Government through the Queen’s Service Medal was brought to the notice of the Ministry of External Affairs on 19th January, 2011. The Ministry requested Sri Lanka’s High Commissioner in Canberra, who is accredited to New Zealand, to raise our concern and displeasure through the New Zealand High Commission in Canberra on the ground that Mr. Thevarajan is an “elected” member of the so-called “Transnational Government of Tamil Eelam (TGTE)” from New Zealand and had consistently agitated for the creation of a mono-ethnic separate state of Tamil Eelam in Sri Lanka. It had also been impressed that this honour conferred upon him would in all likelihood be used for the TGTE’s separatist cause to gain legitimacy.

The initial response received from the New Zealand authorities is that the Queen’s Service Medal is given in recognition of a person’s services to a particular community or field and it is not a sign of legitimacy accorded to the person’s beliefs or activities related to a separatist agenda and the hope expressed that the honour conferred would not be used for that purpose. The position of the Ministry of External Affairs is that we are not satisfied at all with the initial response given by the New Zealand authorities when this matter was raised by our High Commissioner in Canberra who is also accredited to New Zealand.

The TGTE is an illegal organization that has not been recognized by any Government in the world and it should not be recognized by any Government in the world who believes in a civilized society. Giving a recognition medal to a member of the TGTE is, therefore, a violation of international norms. As the Ministry of External Affairs, we deeply regret the act of the New Zealand Government and would reiterate our strong protest at the highest level. So, the position of the Ministry of External Affairs is that. We have already conveyed our displeasure and our concerns through the authorities concerned to the New Zealand Government. As their initial response was not adequate, we are now taking other steps necessary to

1245 1246

[ගරු මහාචාර්ය රාජීව විෙජ්සිංහ මහතා]

2011 අෙපේල් 06

express our displeasure and concern, and also, we condemn this act done by the Government of New Zealand. මූලාසනාරූඪ මන්තීතුමා (தைலைமதாங்கும் உᾠப்பினர் அவர்கள்) (The Presiding Member) Hon. Minister, we could also send them a copy of the Adjournment Motion that has been moved in Parliament today.

ගරු ඩිලාන් ෙපෙර්රා මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ᾊலான் ெபேரரா) (The Hon. Dilan Perera) Yes, Sir.

So, our position, Hon. Member, is that the Ministry of External Affairs has taken notice of this incident and we have already started moving on with the matter. As we are

not satisfied with the initial response by the Government of New Zealand, we are going to take other steps in future at various levels to condemn this action and also to show our displeasure and concern. Thank you very much.

පශ්නය විමසන ලදින්, සභා සම්මත විය. வினா விᾌக்கப்பட்ᾌ ஏற்ᾠக்ெகாள்ளப்பட்டᾐ. Question put, and agreed to.

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව ඊට අනුකූලව අ. භා. 5.30ට, 2011 අෙපේල් 07 වන බහස්පතින්දා අ. භා. 1.00 වන ෙතක් කල් ගිෙය්ය.

அதன்பᾊ பி. ப. 5.30 மணிக்கு பாராᾦமன்றம், 2011 ஏப்பிரல் 07, வியாழக்கிழைம பி.ப. 1.00 மணிவைர ஒத்திைவக்கப்பட்டᾐ.

Adjourned accordingly at 5.30 p.m. until 1.00 p.m. on Thursday, 07th April, 2011.

සැ.යු. ෙමම වාර්තාෙව් අවසාන මුදණය සදහා ස්වකීය නිවැරදි කළ යුතු තැන් දක්වනු රිසි මන්තීන් මින් පිටපතක් ෙගන නිවැරදි කළ යුතු ආකාරය එහි පැහැදිලිව ලකුණු ෙකොට, පිටපත ලැබී ෙදසතියක් ෙනොඉක්මවා හැන්සාඩ් සංස්කාරක ෙවත ලැෙබන ෙසේ එවිය යුතුය.

உᾠப்பினர் இᾠதிப் பதிப்பிற் ெசய்யவிᾞம்ᾗம் பிைழ திᾞத்தங்கைளத் தமᾐ பிரதியில் ெதளிவாகக் குறித்ᾐ அதைனப் பிைழ

දායක මුදල් : පාර්ලිෙම්න්තු විවාද වාර්තාවල වාර්ෂික දායක මිල රු. 2178කි. පිටපතක් ෙගන්වා ගැනීම අවශ්‍ය නම් ගාස්තුව රු. 18.15කි. තැපැල් ගාස්තුව රු. 2.50කි. ෙකොළඹ 6, කිරුළපන, පාමංකඩ පාර, අංක 102, පියසිරි ෙගොඩනැගිල්ෙල් රජෙය් පකාශන කාර්යාංශෙය් අධිකාරී ෙවත සෑම වර්ෂයකම ෙනොවැම්බර් 30 දාට පථම දායක මුදල් ෙගවා ඉදිරි වර්ෂෙය් දායකත්වය ලබා ෙගන විවාද වාර්තා ලබාගත හැකිය. නියමිත දිෙනන් පසුව එවනු ලබන දායක ඉල්ලුම් පත් භාර ගනු ෙනොලැෙබ්. சந்தா ; ஹன்சாட் அதிகார அறிக்ைகயின் வᾞடாந்த சந்தா ᾟபா 2,178. ஹன்சாட் தனிப்பிரதி ᾟபா 18.15. தபாற் ெசலᾫ ᾟபா 2.50. வᾞடாந்த சந்தா ᾙற்பணமாக அத்தியட்சகர், அரசாங்க ெவளியீட்டᾤவலகம், இல. 102, பியசிறி கட்ᾊடம், பாமன்கைட ᾪதி, கிᾞளப்பைன, ெகாᾨம்ᾗ 6 என்ற விலாசத்திற்கு அᾔப்பி பிரதிகைளப் ெபற்ᾠக்ெகாள்ளலாம். ஒவ்ேவாராண்ᾌம் நவம்பர் 30 ஆந் ேததிக்கு ᾙன் சந்தாப்பணம் அᾔப்பப்பட ேவண்ᾌம். பிந்திக் கிைடக்கும் சந்தா விண்ணப்பங்கள் ஏற்ᾠக்ெகாள்ளப்படமாட்டா. Subscriptions : The annual subscription for Official Report of Hansard is Rs. 2,178. A single copy of Hansard is available for Rs. 18.15. (Postage Rs. 2.50) Copies can be obtained by remitting in advance an annual subscription fee to the SUPERINTENDENT, GOVERNMENT PUBLICATIONS BUREAU, No. 102,Piyasiri Building, Pamankada Road, Kirulapone, Colombo 6. The fee should reach him on or before November 30 each year . Late applications for subscriptions will not be accepted. ශී ලංකා රජෙය් මුදණ ෙදපාර්තෙම්න්තුෙව් මුදණය කරන ලදී.
